## Sensitive / disciplinary dockets flagged (0)
_No RECAP docket in this set matched the discipline/bar-matter patterns._ 
(The 2022 Nevada Supreme Court discipline matter lives in `/opinions/`, not RECAP — RECAP is federal PACER only.)

## Notes on data coverage
- RECAP covers federal court filings (PACER). Nevada state criminal/DUI matters are **not** in this set.
- The `attorney`, `firm`, and `party` fields in search results come from elastic indexing and may be sparse. Full party/attorney roster requires follow-up calls to `/dockets/{id}/` and `/dockets/{id}/parties/`.
- Many matches are name collisions (other 'Ogata' defendants). Manual review is needed to separate Garrett-as-counsel from Garrett-as-subject or unrelated-Ogata cases.
